醉红撩乱雪争开,zui'hong'liao'luan'xue'zheng'kai
醉后几行书字小,zui'hou'ji'hang'shu'zi'xiao
醉客快一噉,zui'ke'kuai'yi'dan
醉里穿花满袖风,zui'li'chuan'hua'man'xiu'feng
醉眠聊自适,zui'mian'liao'zi'shi
最思东山烟树色,zui'si'dong'shan'yan'shu'se
最慰章滨父老心,zui'wei'zhang'bin'fu'lao'xin
最嫌尸祝扰庚桑,zui'xian'shi'zhu'rao'geng'sang
醉乡旧业抛来久,zui'xiang'jiu'ye'pao'lai'jiu
醉乡岐路君知否,zui'xiang'qi'lu'jun'zhi'fou
醉消春色爱醅浓,zui'xiao'chun'se'ai'pei'nong
醉吟谁肯伴衰翁,zui'yin'shui'ken'ban'shuai'weng
醉中衣帻任欹斜,zui'zhong'yi'ze'ren'qi'xie
樽酒扁舟慰行役,zun'jiu'pian'zhou'wei'xing'yi
尊形独受众山朝,zun'xing'du'shou'zhong'shan'chao
左车公自迎,zuo'che'gong'zi'ying
坐愁穷海瘴烟霏,zuo'chou'qiong'hai'zhang'yan'fei
坐逮空南亩,zuo'dai'kong'nan'mu
昨登定林山,zuo'deng'ding'lin'shan
坐对高梧倾晓月,zuo'dui'gao'wu'qing'xiao'yue
坐费太官廪,zuo'fei'tai'guan'lin
坐感岁时歌慷慨,zuo'gan'sui'shi'ge'kang'kai
坐间南客送寒醅,zuo'jian'nan'ke'song'han'pei
坐久膝前席,zuo'jiu'xi'qian'xi
坐觉尘襟一夕空,zuo'jue'chen'jin'yi'xi'kong
坐觉尘沙昏远眼,zuo'jue'chen'sha'hun'yuan'yan
坐看闾巷得名声,zuo'kan'lv'xiang'de'ming'sheng
坐看山垄玉崔嵬,zuo'kan'shan'long'yu'cui'wei
坐客多贤豪,zuo'ke'duo'xian'hao
坐恐得空牢,zuo'kong'de'kong'lao
坐旷息烦襟,zuo'kuang'xi'fan'jin
坐论公瑾少能谈,zuo'lun'gong'jin'shao'neng'tan
作么有疏亲,zuo'me'you'shu'qin
坐凭江阁看飞鸿,zuo'ping'jiang'ge'kan'fei'hong
昨日青青尚未齐,zuo'ri'qing'qing'shang'wei'qi
作诗宠行色,zuo'shi'chong'xing'se
坐使千箱有,zuo'shi'qian'xiang'you
坐听楚谣知岁美,zuo'ting'chu'yao'zhi'sui'mei
坐忘唯有一颜回,zuo'wang'wei'you'yi'yan'hui
昨夜南园风雨,zuo'ye'nan'yuan'feng'yu
坐欲肠胃得,zuo'yu'chang'wei'de
坐与文章立太平,zuo'yu'wen'zhang'li'tai'ping
